style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月月更新，是一份关于中国在押政治犯、良心犯的动态报告。至此，本报告历时四年多，每月不辍，期期更新，其中凝聚了许多义工、信息员和编辑长期以来默默无闻的辛劳和奉献。此为第<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">58</span></b>期。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">维权网信息中心每月对大陆当下发生的羁押未判、强迫失踪和已经判刑的各个政治犯、良心犯案例予以汇总、统计，最终编辑和撰写了这一最新月度动态报告。本报告主要关注的对象是所有在押的政治犯、良心犯。包括已被判刑的和羁押未判的——所有我们能够收集到确切信息的政治犯、良心犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告经本网信息义工、信息员和编辑经过近四年的不懈努力的基础上，共收集、整理、编辑了有较为翔实资料的人员名单，共计</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">971</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人。</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">这个数字里内涵着本网所有工作人员在高度风险下的巨大付出。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告之所以能够按时定期发布，并且信息越来越翔实，这也得到了大陆许多人权捍卫者的积极反馈和支持。本网对所有提供信息的朋友，在此一并予以感谢。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告名单人员一旦取保候审、保外就医、无罪释放、回家监视居住、或刑满释放，将从报告正式在押名单中消除，但其简历仍可见当期附录。<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">从报告中我们可以看到：中国大陆政治犯、良心犯中有的被超期羁押，有的被强迫失踪音信全无，有的遭受残暴酷刑和狱中虐待，他们的人权境况极其恶劣。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，遭中共当局迫害致死的曹顺利女士就是这样的一名遭羁押和酷刑的人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年被详细披露的<span lang="EN-US">709</span>案被长期羁押的吴淦、谢阳律师及其他律师所遭遇的十几种残暴酷刑令人发指。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年刘晓波、杨天水、彭明等著名政治犯相继被中共当局迫害致死更是震惊海内外。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">而政治犯良心犯狱中死亡消息还是不断传出，令人骇然！<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月传出哈萨克族政治犯努尔古丽在狱中突然死亡的消息，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被哈萨克州奎屯市法院枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。但努尔古丽仅入狱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天突然死亡。中共当局一直在严密封锁此消息。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉：新疆著名宗教领袖阿卜杜克里姆•阿卜杜外力（维吾尔）在历经五次延长刑期后，其已于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月死于狱中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉：吉林榆树市<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的退休女教师宋兆恒，被关押到榆树市看守所四个多月，被庭审后，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，在看守所被迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京顺义区法轮功学员柳艳梅于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被迫害致死，终年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，她<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月邀请民众旁听对法轮功学员的庭审而被被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在通州看守所遭受惨无人道的虐待折磨而死。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日获悉：四川省攀枝花市<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁的法轮功学员廖健甫，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被绑架至云南省第一监狱第十一分区迫害，家属曾两次探视，得知他血压高到<span lang="EN-US">240</span>，又出现了脑梗，生命垂危。家属多次申请保外就医，监狱拒绝放人。廖健甫于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日晚上九点在云南第一监狱第十一分区被迫害致死。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，著名人权捍卫者纪斯尊先生出狱仅两个月，就在警方看守的病房内死亡，举世震惊。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网持续不断地对政治犯、良心犯境况进行总结和报告，是为了抗议当局以超期羁押、拖延审判、虐待折磨、殴打等各种方式对他们施加酷刑，而在狱中被酷刑虐待折磨是被关押者要经常面对的严酷现实。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网相信，外界坚持不懈的关注将会给狱中受难者以精神和实质的援助。本报告四年多来一直对中共当局使用各种酷刑手段迫害折磨政治犯、良心犯的行径予以的系统揭露，业已引起了海内外各个方面的强烈反响。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网一直在及时更新、统计最新讯息，每月末发布这月度报告，谨以此表达我们对所有失去自由的政治犯、良心犯的关注和牵挂。并以此，告诉全世界不要忘记这些为自由、民主、人权而承担苦难的人们。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，本报告的定期更新和发布，可以直接反映出大陆当下的人权概况——因为一个国家的政治犯、良心犯的境况是这个国家最重要的人权指标之一。本网</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以此</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">揭示中国大陆当下恶劣的人权概况与良心犯、政治犯的悲惨处境，力求唤起国际社会对中国在押政治犯、良心犯的记忆，并予以持续不断的关注和呼吁，直至他们获得自由。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本网认为，定期将良心犯、政治犯的姓名和境况公诸于世，是我们能给予这些受难者以实际而有效支持的一种方式。我们深知，没有比被人们的遗忘更令这些良心犯、政治犯感到绝望和痛苦的事情。因此，我们必须肩负起这项工作，乃至是使命。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">最后，我们深知这份报告虽经同仁的共同努力，但仍然只是冰山之一角，仍然是一份不完全的报告，这需要我们的继续努力！</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日发布。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">（一）本期报告概述：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告全文共计<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">27</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千余字</b>，分<span lang="EN-US">8</span>部分发布。报告政治犯、良心犯名单分羁押未判和已经判刑两大类，共计</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">966</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人。报告对羁押未判的<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">340</span></b>人名单按区域统计的概述；对已判刑的<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">626</span></b>人是按判刑期的年限长短（即由死刑正在核准、死缓、无期徒刑至有期徒刑）进行统计排列概述。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">为便于人们查询，本网依据《维权网：中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》为顺序刊发在押政治犯、良心犯的简介。索引是以姓名拼音顺序排列（<span lang="EN-US">ABCDEFG....WXYZ</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本报告竭力就包括汉、藏、维、哈萨克、回、蒙古、朝鲜、满等中国大陆多族裔政治犯、良心犯在内的信息进行收集和编撰，力求全面真实反映当前中国大陆政治犯、良心犯的恶劣的生存境遇。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告虽经本网信息中心认真核查，并得到中国大陆许多人权捍卫者协助，但仍因条件所限，无法做到适时、准确统计全部在押政治犯、良心犯信息，若有纰漏之处和补充信息，敬请读者指正，并尽可能知会本网。本网邮箱：<span lang="EN-US">wqw2011@gmail.com<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告表明：中共当局对在押政治犯、良心犯的指控及判罪罪名多达<span lang="EN-US">46</span>种：<span lang="EN-US">46.</span>“从事非法宗教活动罪”。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告表明：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、中国大陆新疆地区对维吾尔族等穆斯林的实施普遍的集中营式的所谓“转化学习班”。</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">在新疆中共当局令人恐惧地不经任何法律程序，肆意剥夺一个族群的人身自由。因新疆严密的信息封锁，我们无法确知具体的人数，有估算应该数以百万计。目前已经透露出，许多在集中营式的关押过程中死亡的事件。本报告所涉及的数名不知去向的维吾尔人应该是在此类集中营中。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、中国大陆酷刑及虐待依然普遍而严重，很多政治犯、良心犯健康状况令人担忧；</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">继上期报告之后，截至目前，依然存有大量在押政治犯、良心犯、人权捍卫者因狱中生存条件甚差或遭遇严重不公及狱警暴力殴打、恶意刁难等，以致健康严重受损，甚至危机生命等事实；很多人在押期间都遭受过刑讯逼供、酷刑或长期非人虐待、被强关精神病院，甚至被酷刑致死、被长期监禁和被延期监禁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈萨克族曾押政治犯努尔古丽判刑后仅转狱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天突然死亡。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月因质疑清真食品与猪肉混合出售而被刑拘，后被以涉“宣扬、散布、传播宗教极端、暴力恐怖思想”等罪批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被哈萨克州奎屯市法院枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">16</span>年。中共当局在严密封锁此消息。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2018</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月又获悉：新疆著名宗教领袖阿卜杜克里姆•阿卜杜外力（维吾尔）在历经五次延长刑期后，其已于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月死于狱中；据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年其家人在最后一次探望他时，看见其只能坐轮椅，关节肿胀。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，著名人权捍卫者纪斯尊先生出狱仅两个月，就在警方看守的病房内死亡，举世震惊。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、对宗教人士的镇压仍在持续；</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">从本网现有收集的在押良心犯资料来看，继江泽民、胡温之后，至今习近平主政时期，中共当局对宗教人士的迫害愈发严重。就全国情势来看，尤其是对各地区、各族裔民众宗教信仰自由的打击、逼迫情况加大了严打力度。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年底，四川成都<span lang="EN-US">12.9</span>秋雨教案，是中共当局对基督教的最大镇压事件，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月覃德富长老获刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，而王怡牧师则遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、对法轮功的迫害没有丝毫减弱。</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中共当局对法轮功信仰者的残酷迫害和镇压从未停止，迫害法轮功的活动越发猖獗，不断有法轮功人士被抓捕和判刑，法轮功仍是当下遭受镇压最严厉的群体之一。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦皇岛法轮功学员马桂兰，女，六十多岁，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被秦皇岛市开发区珠江道派出所抓捕。送进秦皇岛市拘留所，行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。到<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，马桂兰由<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天的行政拘留突转为刑事拘留。大约在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，突然传出马桂兰在秦皇岛看守所被迫害致死。而且在这不到一个月期间内，看守所还有<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人也离奇死亡。进入<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，吉林榆树市<span lang="EN-US">76</span>岁的退休女教师宋兆恒，被关押到榆树市看守所四个多月，被庭审后，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，在看守所被迫害致死。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京顺义区法轮功学员柳艳梅于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被迫害致死，终年<span lang="EN-US">52</span>岁，她<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月邀请民众旁听对法轮功学员的庭审而被被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在通州看守所遭受惨无人道的虐待折磨而死。</span></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">由此<span lang="EN-US">4</span>点可见，自习近平主政以来，中共当局在加紧镇压各地人权捍卫者、底层民众的基本维权、政治民主、宗教信仰自由的诸多诉求过程中，打压行动已变得愈发目无法律、蛮横霸道、为所欲为。许多在押政治犯、良心犯案例已一再表明，当局对外宣称的所谓“依法治国”仅限于口头，是对中国老百姓和国际社会的瞒哄欺骗，它显然与真正意义上民主诉求的“宪政之路”南辕北辙。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">而且，为进一步控制人们的自由信仰意识，进一步镇压觉醒中的人民捍卫权利和追求民主自由的行动，当局经常成立所谓“专案组”，公然挑衅和藐视司法正义程序，酷刑虐待频然，手段极其残忍卑劣，使得许多身陷囹圄的在押政治犯、良心犯、人权捍卫者、宗教信仰人士毫无基本的人权保障和法律尊严。这一不争事实亟待让国际社会进一步了解，并吁请国际社会给予中国大陆空前糟糕的人权状况尽多的关注及实际干预，坚决谴责酷刑的存在，敦促中共当局切实兑现已签署的《联合国国际反酷刑公约》，释放所有政治犯、良心犯和人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">以上这些情况都会在以下名录简介中逐一披露。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本期报告中录入的在押政治犯、良心犯共计</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast;">966</span></b></span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373588;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk507373498;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; minor-fareast;">人，其中，羁押未判的<span lang="EN-US">340</span>人，已经判刑的<span lang="EN-US">626</span>人。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br minor-fareast;">为了更方便人们查询本网统计的在押政治犯、良心犯的名单，本网每期随《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯月度报告》一起发布《中国大陆在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引》。本索引将本期报告所统计的人员名单，以人员姓名拼音字母排序（<span lang="EN-US">A</span>、<span lang="EN-US">B</span>、<span lang="EN-US">C</span>、<span lang="EN-US">D</span>、<span lang="EN-US">E</span>、<span lang="EN-US">F.....X</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Y</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Z</span>）。查询者可依据姓名的第一个拼音字母，即可查询到相关人员姓名，而其简介均可在报告中查找到。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">中国大陆<span lang="EN-US">966</span>名在押政治犯、良心犯名单索引简介<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></div><div align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">A.<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿贾贾（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜（维吾尔）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺觉尼（藏）、阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿亚桑扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾则孜•艾买提（维）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安然、昂扎（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">奥坎（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿布杜热扎克•夏木西丁（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊宁市人，伊宁市克拜克玉孜村农民，曾当过木工，维吾尔名<span lang="EN-US">Abdurazzak Shamseden</span>，新疆著名持不同政见者。<span lang="EN-US">1994</span>年曾因其胞弟萨迪尔丁·夏木西丁<span lang="EN-US">(Sadirdin Shamseden)</span>发起一个旨在解决维吾尔人酗酒及毒品泛滥等社会问题的民间草根运动（又叫“麦西莱普活动”），其亦参与其中。尽管几年间该运动发展日益壮大，覆盖了几乎整个伊宁周边地区，但终因碰触到中共高层的敏感神经，引起中共新疆当局的极度恐慌，遂遭强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年麦西莱普活动被政府明令禁止；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日新疆伊宁发生维吾尔族市民大规模抗议游行示威，虽被很快强力镇压，但之后伊宁地区的胡迪亚玉孜村又发生了警民冲突，且又有六人被军警枪杀，因其外甥哈穆提•莫哈买提<span lang="EN-US">(Hemmat Muhemmet)</span>是警民冲突中死亡青年之一，所以其亦被怀疑参与其中。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被当局抓捕，并被指控与<span lang="EN-US">2.5</span>伊宁抗议示威及本次警民冲突有关；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月其被伊宁市中级法院以“分裂国家罪”判处无期徒刑，剥夺政治权利终身；其不服上诉，二审后依然维持原判；据悉其惨遭刑讯逼供和极端非人待遇；审讯和审判期间，几乎所有人道权利及法律基本权利均被剥夺，既无任何法律代理，又不准与家属见面，其家属不仅没有接到审判日通知，判决书中也无确切审判日期，亲属只是在上诉截止日前三天，才由小道消息获此判决信息。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿布拉江·阿乌提·阿有普（<span lang="EN-US">Ablajan Awut Ayup</span>）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">维吾尔族、新疆和田人，是极受维吾尔人欢迎的维吾尔青年歌手，因为颂歌维吾尔人而被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被新疆当局重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年徒刑。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿尔恒•巴杂尔别克（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿里木江•依米提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区哈密市人，原英资企业新疆佳尔豪氏食品有限公司喀什分公司经理，曾信仰伊斯兰教，后改信基督教，喀什地区基督教传道人，中国在押良心犯。曾因在新疆喀什地区举办基督教家庭教会活动，并积极传播基督教义和发展基督教徒等，触碰到了中共当局的意识形态底线，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，被新疆喀什市民族宗教事务局认定为“<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年以来，以工作名义，在喀什地区非法从事宗教渗透活动，在维吾尔族群众中传播基督教，散发宗教宣传品，发展基督教徒”；<span lang="EN-US"> 2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，喀什市警方突然将其带走，随即以“涉嫌煽动分裂国家罪”和 “向境外非法提供国家秘密罪”将其刑事拘留，关押于新疆喀什市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被当地检察院正式批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，新疆喀什中级法院对其进行了秘密开庭审理，后因证据不足，被法庭退回当地警方补充侦查；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被喀市地区中级法院再次秘审，被以“向境外人员非法提供国家秘密罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被新疆自治区高级法院重审，最终仍以<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年（ “绝密”级别量刑）维持原判。目前在新疆维吾尔自治区第三监狱服刑；据悉，在关押期间其曾遭酷刑毒打，被送进喀什农三师医院救治；其妻探监亦由每个月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>分钟探视时间减少到每三个月一次仅<span lang="EN-US">10</span>分钟；截止<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，因当地警方和社区管理部门不予开具准许探视证明，其妻探监再遭刁难。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿贾贾（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州阿坝县麦尔玛乡第一大队人，原格尔登寺僧人，人权捍卫者、政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，曾因在格尔登寺僧人洛桑彭措自焚抗议时呼喊口号而遭被捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年多，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年刑满释放。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被警方突然再次抓走，自此失联，后从非官方渠道打听得知，其被警方指控涉嫌“为达赖喇嘛八十寿辰祈寿”而遭逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被四川省阿坝藏族羌族自治州中级法院以不详罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。据悉，其被捕至获刑前一直毫无音讯，且当局拒绝其聘请代理律师为其辩护。目前关押服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿斯哈·阿孜提别克（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族，原伊宁市飞机场路<span lang="EN-US">61</span>号北苑别墅区居民，前伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县粮食局官员，原伊犁哈萨克自治州政府移民管理局退休干部，哈萨克国籍公民，中国在押政治犯。因其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局工作期间，接触过伊犁河流域水利工程的移民搬迁工作，熟知伊犁河是中哈国际河流和涉伊犁河流域相关水利工程项目，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月又与哈萨克共和国驻中国乌鲁木齐签证代办处副主任达尼亚尔·赛力克巴耶夫<span lang="EN-US">(SERIKBAYEV DANIYAR)</span>相结识，遂遭中共新疆当局的高度警觉、监控与强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，其已移民至哈萨克斯坦国（以下简称“哈国”），并于同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月加入哈国国籍；但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被强行驾车驶入中国霍尔果斯口岸至哈国国际市场路段的哈国境内自由贸易区的中国新疆警方跨境绑架，自此失联；尽管其已移民并加入哈国国籍，但仍被中共政府视为新疆居民，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被霍城县警方以同罪由转正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其案被霍城县检察院以“间谍罪”和“诈骗罪”起诉至新疆维吾尔自治区高级法院伊犁哈萨克自治州分院，指控其曾在伊犁州政府移民管理局任职期间，结识了哈国民族安全委员会成员，并按其要求对伊犁河流域水利设施及河流进行拍照，提供水利设施信息等，该行为触犯了中国法律，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被该法院秘密审判，以“间谍罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，以“诈骗罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，数罪并罚，最后执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。目前被羁押于伊犁哈萨克自治州霍城县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿提开姆•茹孜（维吾尔）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1992</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆维吾尔自治区人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Atikem Rozi</span>，著名维吾尔学者伊力哈木•土赫提的学生<span lang="EN-US">,</span>“维吾尔在线”网站义工。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年，因个人护照申请连续三次被当局以政治原因而拒发（尽管其无任何政治不良记录），随将其遭遇发布到新浪微博上，之后各大媒体如《都市北京》<span lang="EN-US">(Metro Beijing)</span>、“维吾尔在线”和《环球时报》等官媒便竞相刊发或转载了涉及其本人与其他维吾尔人申请护照时遭遇双重标准的文章，引发社会热议；此一举动因惹怒了中共当局，并遭到当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被乌鲁木齐警方以在“媒体上辩论”为由传唤，被审问<span lang="EN-US">6</span>小时后才被释放，两天之后又遭威吓骚扰；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日因其多次使用<span lang="EN-US">twitter,facebook</span>以及新浪微博等网站发布文章和讯息，并利用网媒广泛寻找被失踪多日的男友穆塔力普•伊明，随被以曾是伊力哈木•土赫提的学生、曾是“维吾尔在线”网站义工为由被北京警方传唤，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被乌鲁木齐市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日其案在乌鲁木齐巿中级法院开庭审理，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被乌鲁木齐巿中级法院以“积极参与分裂国家犯罪集团罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3-8</span>年，最多将于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出狱。服刑监狱不详。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿旺觉尼（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生年月不详，籍贯不详（只知藏区僧人），西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院经师，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并长期在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺密宗学院研习、进修；因曾长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其主要弟子之一，遂被哲蚌寺密宗学院立为经师（即精通佛教经藏的僧人，又称佛教讲经诵经的师父）；又由于其受教尊师兰林仁波切是深受藏民普遍敬重的哲蚌寺喇嘛，地位、声望及影响力并非由政府任命，因此被当局视为异己予以排挤、管控，其因与之交往甚密，故而亦成为当局长期监控打压的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，因藏区发生以僧侣为主的大规模抗议示威活动，以期达到让中共当局真正实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并呼吁准许达赖喇嘛回国返乡等政治诉求，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其所在哲蚌寺<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦参与其中，致使抗议行动很快扩展至整个拉萨市区及四川、青海等藏区；针对此，西藏当局很快派遣大批持枪武警予以极端管控，双方发生严重对峙与冲突，随后即有众多僧侣被抓捕，其余人等被遣返寺庙严加看守；尽管此前其并未参与游行抗议，但是，<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其仍被拉萨市警方以涉嫌“参与抗议活动”抓捕，自此长期失联；另有二名哲蚌寺好友、学者僧侣亦被一同抓捕；后被拉萨市检察院转正式批捕，罪由竟是“未能阻止哲蚌寺僧人举行大规模抗议行动”；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在被长期羁押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，被拉萨市中级法院以不详罪名密判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，因长期失联，其狱中具体境况均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿吾勒别克·努尔加合蒲（哈萨克）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US">Ayelbek Nurzhahp</span>，伊犁州昭苏县阿克达拉镇清真寺伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），中国在押良心犯。早年曾就读于伊犁特克斯县宗教学校，毕业后被官方指定为昭苏县清真寺的伊玛目（即宗教仪式领祷人或主持），管辖服务于当地<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个清真寺；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，曾多次到哈萨克共和国（简称哈国）访问；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因感觉新疆政治气氛欠佳而将妻子和两个孩子送到哈国，其本人亦打算将自己在新疆的不动产（包括牲畜等）变卖后移民哈国，不料被中共新疆当局知晓，遂被警方以“不准移民哈国”为由抓捕，并遭威胁让其全家（含其妻子和孩子）务必返回国内生活；其全家虽按要求照办，但<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日仍被昭苏县警方突然抓走，并被关押在当地的政治再教育营；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被昭苏县警方以“全家要移民哈国”为罪由正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州昭苏县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，罪名不详，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2042</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日；据悉，在被判决时，法院竟称让其“自己选择罪名，然后给判刑”；其妻、其弟被送政治再教育营教育，后亦被以同罪由各判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年。目前在生产建设兵团农七师高泉监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿亚桑扎（藏族）：青海省果洛州牧民。</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阿亚桑扎是因为上访被抓捕的，<span lang="EN-US"> 2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，因为他经牧民选举当上牧委会主任，却被官方把<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年已经了结的案件，重新拿出来说事把他抓捕冤屈判刑一年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，上诉也被维持原判。阿亚桑扎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日下午在果洛州高速路口上访途中，被公安人员抓捕连夜送到西宁次日送到了乐都区看守所。阿亚桑扎对自己被关押到离果洛州<span lang="EN-US">600</span>公里外的看守所感到不可理解，认为这是官方对他的一种折磨。他被抓时正在带领大家控告相关人员贪污犯罪的事情进展情况，要大家继续坚持控告下去。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，阿亚桑扎被当局判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑。阿亚桑扎等所谓涉恶案件开庭两天当庭宣判，其对获刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年当庭表示不服提起上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">艾则孜•艾买提（维吾尔）</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">47</span>岁，新疆阿克苏地区维族教长。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月因皮山县一个村市集从事宗教教学活动，被当地公安局拘捕，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被判入狱<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安然：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">本名崔浩新、济南回民作家、诗人（即推友<span lang="EN-US">@ismaelan </span>）。安然现年<span lang="EN-US">41</span>岁的安然曾在官方刊物发表过自己的作品，其中有作品被收录到中国作家协会编选的“新时期少数民族文学选”。他早前发表的《我的诗歌志》，记录其诗歌生涯中有一大部分为关注新疆的内容。此前<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月曾因在推特转发和发布的有关新疆“再教育营”的报道和文字等言论遭警方抓捕，后都有惊无险获释。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日即农历春节除夕夜遭济南警方刑事拘留，罪名是寻衅滋事。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">昂扎（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人处以重刑，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等严打措施；在此背景下，昂扎所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方以涉嫌“参与抗议示威”，“秘密组织相关人员在家里召开会议”等罪由刑拘，后被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><div class="MsoNormal"><br /></div><div class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">奥坎（哈萨克）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">出生不详，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，伊犁哈萨克自治州阿尔泰地区哈巴河县清真寺阿訇（即伊斯兰宗教事务主持人），伊斯兰知名宗教领袖，中国在押良心犯。近年来，因新疆地区局势日益紧张，中共当局加强了对新疆各民族在宗教信仰上的高压管控手段和措施，哈萨克族人也不例外；这期间，因奥坎是阿尔泰地区哈萨克族群中知名宗教界领袖，影响力大，遂当局严密监控，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年又因其按照本民族及宗教习俗为死者做了传统的祷告仪式，被当地警方偷拍，随后即以此问罪，被抓刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，其被阿尔泰地区哈巴河县法院以不具名罪名秘判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。目前羁押或服刑地点不详。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></div><br /></div>
</div>
